<P STYLE="font: 16pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 16pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B><U>THE COCA-COLA COMPANY ANNOUNCES SENIOR<BR>
LEADERSHIP APPOINTMENTS</U></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B><I>Creates New Chief Growth Officer
Role </I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B><I>Elevates Innovation and Information
Technology Functions</I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B><I>Three Senior Functional Leaders
Announce Retirements</I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B><I>&nbsp;</I></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0 0 10pt"><B>ATLANTA, March 23, 2017</B> &ndash; The Coca-Cola
Company today announced a number of senior leadership appointments to drive its ongoing transformation into a growth-oriented,
consumer-centered, total beverage company. Key changes, which will be effective when President and COO James Quincey becomes Chief
Executive Officer on May 1, include:</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 11pt/normal Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 21.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 18pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 11.5pt">&#183;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 11.5pt">Combining Global Marketing, Customer and Commercial
Leadership, and Strategy into one combined function under the leadership of a new <B>Chief Growth Officer</B> to drive growth across
five strategic beverage categories.</FONT></TD></TR>                                                    <TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD>&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 11pt/normal Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 21.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 18pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 11.5pt">&#183;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 11.5pt">Appointing a <B>Chief Innovation Officer</B> to
elevate Global Research &amp; Development into a standalone innovation function reporting directly to the CEO. This represents
the increased importance of innovation to the company&rsquo;s growth plans.</FONT></TD></TR>                                                                                            <TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD>&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 11pt/normal Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 21.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 18pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 11.5pt">&#183;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 11.5pt">Positioning the <B>Information Technology</B> function
as a direct report to the CEO given the importance of digitization as a growth enabler for the company&rsquo;s business.</FONT></TD></TR>                                                                                                                                         <TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD>&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 11pt/normal Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 8pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 21.35pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 18pt"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 11.5pt">&#183;</FONT></TD><TD><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 11.5pt">Combining key global transactional and expertise
services into an expanded and reconstituted <B>Integrated Services</B> organization that will primarily focus on financial, procurement
and associate shared services. </FONT></TD></TR>                                                <TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD>&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD><TD>&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&ldquo;Today&rsquo;s organizational announcement is another
building block in our company&rsquo;s transformational journey,&rdquo; Quincey said. &ldquo;We are moving quickly to structure
our organization for faster growth and to ensure we can respond to the fast-changing needs of our consumers, customers, system
and associates around the world. Each of the leaders named today is highly capable and understands our clear mandate for change,
and I look forward to partnering with them as we transform our business for the future.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0 0 10pt">The changes support work already under way to create
a leaner, more agile corporate organization that is focused on strategy, governance and vital strategic initiatives, such as innovation
and portfolio growth through leading brands and categories. They also follow changes made by Quincey to the company&rsquo;s international
operations leadership team last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B><U></U></B></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Silver 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><TD STYLE="width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: right; color: red">Page 2</P>



<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B><U>Senior Leadership Appointments</U></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0 0 10pt">Leaders assuming new or expanded responsibility in
the organization and reporting directly to Quincey, effective May 1, include:</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left">
    <TD STYLE="width: 80%"><B>Francisco Crespo</B>, who currently serves as President of the Mexico business unit, will fill the
    newly created role of Chief Growth Officer. A 28-year company veteran, Crespo will lead the company&rsquo;s global marketing,
    corporate strategy, and customer and commercial leadership teams to create a consolidated team with a clear mandate for driving
    global growth. This role will lead the evolving category cluster model focused around five beverage categories: sparkling,
    juice/dairy/plant-based, tea and coffee, water and enhanced waters and energy. <B>Julie Hamilton, </B>Chief Customer and Commercial
    Leadership Officer, and the Corporate Strategy and Planning and Global Marketing leadership teams will report to the Chief
    Growth Officer.</TD>
    <TD STYLE="width: 20%; text-align: left; vertical-align: top; padding-left: 6pt"><IMG SRC="image_002.jpg" ALT="Text Box:  &#13;&#10;Crespo&#13;&#10;&#13;&#10;" STYLE="height: 144px; width: 156px">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE>


<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>


<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0 0 10pt">Crespo is uniquely qualified for this role, having
successfully led the expansion of Coca-Cola&rsquo;s total beverage portfolio in each of the key Latin America markets where he
has worked. Since 2013, he has overseen the continued expansion of products and brands in Mexico, which is one of the company&rsquo;s
most important international business units.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">To read Crespo&rsquo;s biography, click <U>here</U>.</P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left">
    <TD STYLE="width: 20%; padding-right: 6pt"><IMG SRC="image_003.jpg" ALT="Text Box:  &#13;&#10;Long&#13;&#10;" STYLE="height: 174px; width: 141px">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 80%"><P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0"><B>Robert Long</B>, currently Vice President, Research and Development, will become a direct report to the CEO as Chief Innovation Officer. This move is indicative of Coca-Cola&rsquo;s increased focus on accelerating the growth of its consumer-centric brand portfolio with hundreds of new products and continued innovation in beverages, packaging, ingredients and other areas of the business around the world.</P>
                                                                  <P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">&nbsp;</P>
                                                                  <P STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0">To read Long&rsquo;s
                                         biography, click <U>here</U>.&nbsp;</P></TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left">
    <TD STYLE="width: 80%"><P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>Barry Simpson,</B> currently Senior Vice President and
Chief Information Officer, will remain in his role but be elevated as a direct report to the CEO to increase visibility and focus
on efforts to digitize all aspects of the company&rsquo;s business. Barry became CIO last fall and oversees all of the company&rsquo;s
global information technology strategy, services and operations.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">To read Simpson&rsquo;s biography, click <U>here</U>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P></TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 20%; padding-left: 6pt"><IMG SRC="image_004.jpg" ALT="Text Box:  &#13;&#10;Simpson&#13;&#10;&#13;&#10;" STYLE="height: 160px; width: 157px">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>


<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left">
    <TD STYLE="width: 20%; padding-right: 6pt"><IMG SRC="image_005.jpg" ALT="Text Box:  &#13;&#10;Waller&#13;&#10;" STYLE="height: 161px; width: 141px">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 80%">
<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>Kathy
Waller</B>, currently Executive Vice President and Chief Financial Officer, will assume expanded responsibility for the company&rsquo;s
strategic governance areas as Executive Vice President, Chief Financial Officer and President, Enabling Services. In addition to
the Global Finance organization, the Global Technical team led by <B>Dr. Ed Hays</B>, a newly created Integrated Services team,
which will be led by <B>Robin Moore</B>, and a new Business Transformation team to be led by <B>Mark Eppert</B> will report to
Waller. The Integrated Services team will focus on financial, procurement and associate shared services while the Business Transformation
team will be responsible for driving the changes needed to implement the company&rsquo;s new operating model, including productivity
and zero-based work.</P>
&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Silver 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><TD STYLE="width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: right; color: red">Page 3</P>



<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">Moore, currently Chief of Internal Audit, joined the company in
1995 and has held numerous roles of increasing responsibility within the Finance organization. She led the establishment of the
company&rsquo;s global finance shared service capability within the company&rsquo;s Global Business Services (GBS) organization.
She will replace <B>Ann Taylor</B>, currently President of GBS, who will retire from the company after a successful 32-year career.
Taylor&rsquo;s leadership in the formation and growth of the GBS organization since 2009 has been instrumental in creating the
foundation to expand shared services capabilities through a new Integrated Services organization.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">Eppert, who currently serves as Chief Financial and Supply Chain
Officer for Coca-Cola North America, will join Waller&rsquo;s team to lead Global Business Transformation. With nearly 25 years
of Coca-Cola experience, Eppert is uniquely qualified for his new role having held key leadership positions in Coca-Cola Refreshments
and in the North America business unit, including Foodservice and On-Premise, the Sparkling Category business unit and the Columbus,
Ohio Syrup Branch. <B>Brent Hastie</B>, <FONT STYLE="color: windowtext">currently Senior Vice President, Corporate Strategy and
Planning, will succeed Eppert as Chief Financial and Supply Chain Officer for Coca-Cola North America. Hastie joined the company
in 2006 and has held numerous finance, strategy, commercial and brand leadership roles in Corporate, Coca-Cola Refreshments and
the North America Group. He will report to Sandy Douglas, </FONT>Executive Vice President and President, Coca-Cola North America<FONT STYLE="color: windowtext">.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">To read Waller&rsquo;s biography, click <U>here</U>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left">
    <TD STYLE="width: 80%">
<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>Jennifer Mann, </B>currently Chief of Staff to Quincey, will
become Chief People Officer. Coca-Cola&rsquo;s long-term growth and success is dependent on investing in and developing its people
and strengthening the talent pipeline. Mann will lead efforts to drive cultural change throughout the organization and will continue
to serve as Quincey&rsquo;s Chief of Staff.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">To read Mann&rsquo;s biography, click <U>here</U>.</P></TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 20%; padding-left: 6pt"><IMG SRC="image_006.jpg" ALT="Text Box:  &#13;&#10;Mann&#13;&#10;" STYLE="height: 156px; width: 141px">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/normal Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>


<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left">
    <TD STYLE="width: 20%; padding-right: 6pt"><IMG SRC="image_007.jpg" ALT="Text Box:  &#13;&#10;Perez&#13;&#10;" STYLE="height: 160px; width: 141px">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 80%">
<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>Bea Perez</B>, currently Vice President and Chief Sustainability
Officer, will become Chief Public Affairs, Communications and Sustainability Officer. In this new role, Perez will leverage the
important external stakeholder work done in Public Affairs and Communications, sustainability and partnerships in a more strategic,
integrated and holistic way.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">To read Perez&rsquo;s biography, click <U>here</U>.</P></TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B><U>Senior Leadership Retirements</U></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">In addition to today&rsquo;s appointments, three long-time senior
functional leaders have chosen to retire from the company. Each will assist in the transition of their functions and serve as advisers
to Quincey until their retirements.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 3 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Silver 1pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><TD STYLE="width: 100%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: right; color: red">Page 4</P>



<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left">
    <TD STYLE="width: 80%">
<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>Marcos
de Quinto</B>, Executive Vice President and Chief Marketing Officer, will retire after a nearly 35-year Coca-Cola career. De Quinto
moved to Atlanta to assume the CMO position in January 2015 and has been responsible for a resurgence in the quality of Coca-Cola advertising, including the successful One Brand marketing strategy, global &ldquo;Taste the Feeling&rdquo; campaign and
new visual identity system for Trademark Coca-Cola launched last year, as well as a full-scale, global relaunch of Fanta rolling
out this year. De Quinto also led work to improve marketing productivity, which enabled significant reinvestments in marketing
spend and supporting results in the company&rsquo;s growth.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">To read de Quinto&rsquo;s biography, click <U>here</U>.</P></TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 20%; padding-left: 6pt"><IMG SRC="image_008.jpg" ALT="Text Box:  &#13;&#10;de Quinto&#13;&#10;" STYLE="height: 160px; width: 141px">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>


<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left">
    <TD STYLE="width: 20%; padding-right: 6pt"><IMG SRC="image_009.jpg" ALT="Text Box:  &#13;&#10;Eberly&#13;&#10;" STYLE="height: 161px; width: 141px">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 80%">
<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>Ceree Eberly, </B>Senior Vice President and Chief People
Officer, will retire after a 27-year Coca-Cola career. Since becoming Chief People Officer in 2009, Eberly has led significant
improvements in the company&rsquo;s people and talent processes, including the recent launch of a new Performance Enablement system
and ongoing enhancements to training and retention programs for top talent in the company&rsquo;s leadership pipeline.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">To read Eberly&rsquo;s biography, click <U>here</U>.</P></TD></TR>
</TABLE>


<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; width: 100%">
<TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left">
    <TD STYLE="width: 80%">
<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>Clyde
Tuggle</B>, Senior Vice President and Chief Public Affairs and Communications Officer, will retire after a 28-year Coca-Cola career.
Since assuming his current position in 2009, he has brought a new way of thinking to the Public Affairs and Communications function,
driving increased proactive engagement with a wide array of external stakeholders around the world. Among his many accomplishments
in Public Affairs, Tuggle put in place a strong, connected global Public Affairs and Communications leadership team, and built
the company&rsquo;s social and digital capability and presence, including the creation of Coca-Cola Journey, the company&rsquo;s
award-winning online digital magazine.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">To read Tuggle&rsquo;s biography, click <U>here</U>.</P></TD>
    <TD STYLE="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 20%; padding-left: 6pt"><IMG SRC="image_010.jpg" ALT="Text Box:  &#13;&#10;Tuggle&#13;&#10;" STYLE="height: 153px; width: 141px">&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&ldquo;We enter this next chapter of our history on the shoulders
of so many great leaders who have come before us,&rdquo; Quincey continued. &ldquo;We are grateful to Marcos, Ceree and Clyde for
their nearly 90 years of combined service to the company, and we salute their legacy of strong leadership and wise counsel. We
wish them each the best as they retire.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B><U></U></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 8pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: right; color: red">Page 5</P>



<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B><U>About The Coca-Cola Company</U></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0 0 10pt">The Coca-Cola Company (NYSE: KO) is the world's largest
beverage company, refreshing consumers with more than 500 sparkling and still brands and nearly 3,900 beverage choices. Led by
Coca-Cola, one of the world's most valuable and recognizable brands, our company&rsquo;s portfolio features 21 billion-dollar brands,
19 of which are available in reduced-, low- or no-calorie options. Our billion-dollar brands include Diet Coke, Coca-Cola Zero,
Fanta, Sprite, Dasani, vitaminwater, Powerade, Minute Maid, Simply, Del Valle, Georgia and Gold Peak. Through the world's largest
beverage distribution system, we are the No. 1 provider of both sparkling and still beverages. More than 1.9 billion servings of
our beverages are enjoyed by consumers in more than 200 countries each day. With an enduring commitment to building sustainable
communities, our company is focused on initiatives that reduce our environmental footprint, create a safe, inclusive work environment
for our associates, and enhance the economic development of the communities where we operate. Together with our bottling partners,
we rank among the world's top 10 private employers with more than 700,000 system associates. For more information, visit Coca-Cola
Journey at www.coca-colacompany.com, follow us on Twitter at twitter.com/CocaColaCo, visit our blog, Coca-Cola Unbottled, at www.coca-
colablog.com or find us on LinkedIn at www.linkedin.com/company/the-coca-cola-company.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center">###</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11.5pt/normal Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"></P>
